<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP215883" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_11">

</th>
<td><i>Voices</i>: 5 haut-dessus, 3 hautes-contres, 2 tailles, 4 basses + mixed chorus (AATB)<br /><i>Orchestra</i>: 2 flutes, 2 oboes + strings + continuo
</td></tr></table>
